### 🧠 **OpenAI Codex – Major product evolution**

**Codex continues rolling out substantial enhancements** beyond the original launch:"  
• Recent updates include a **revamped Codex CLI** tuned for *agentic coding workflows*, with richer tool use, progress tracking (to‑do lists), and enhanced modes for approval and workspace access.  
• A **new Codex IDE extension** allows tight integration into VS Code (and forks like Cursor), enabling cloud task previews, context‑preserving work, and smoother local‑cloud handoffs.  
• **Cloud agent improvements** boost task container caching (median completion times slashed ~90 %) and dynamic environment setup, including internet‑based dependency installs.  
• Codex now supports **code review capabilities** that reason over entire codebases, post results directly to GitHub PRs, and enable explicit review commands like `@codex review`.  
⇒ This set of upgrades — CLI, IDE extension, cloud perf, and code‑review — qualifies as a **major evolution of the Codex platform**. citeturn0search1
